  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_2639f513-2c84-4fdd-af2b-ab3e94e8cd4f'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initializeSiwa();

<span id="freeTextContainer1813678154137331596">A deadly game of hide and seek. <br/><br/>With blood still on her hands, Samantha Matthews is on the run, running from dark secrets and a man she prays to God will never find her.   <span id="freeText1813678154137331596" style="display:none">A deadly game of hide and seek. <br /><br />With blood still on her hands, Samantha Matthews is on the run, running from dark secrets and a man she prays to God will never find her. Running and hiding, just to stay alive. She had no choice but to run, to leave, to hide and forget about her life before. When Samantha believes she's gained enough distance from her past and her demons, she stops running, hoping to find her future in the heavily wooded area of the Adirondack Mountains, a place she never expected to encounter a man with secrets as dark and as sordid as hers. <br /><br />Kade Grayson is hiding, not from the demons after him, but from himself and from the entire outside world, wishing every day he could have just died. Arrogant and domineering, he’s tormented and terrorized by his past, seeing nothing good for his future. With the ghosts of his past still haunting him, he has exiled himself to a life of solitude, only living for his words and through his stories.<br /><br />Until her.<br /><br />An undeniable attraction, turns into hate and then ultimately obsession, an obsession that grows into a powerful story of love and redemption.<br /><br />Will the bond they have begun to build between them grow stronger than the tragedies that have scarred both of their lives? Or will they allow their demons to consume them?</span>

      });
      $('span_class_gr-hyperlink_more_filters_span_tip_151').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

//]]>
</script>    </div>

    <div class="section firstReview">
      

<div id="review_812006679" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/812006679" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/812006679?book_show_action=true">Jan 04, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Christy by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/1609377-kara">Kara</a>
  </div>


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer812006679" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer814212953743245845"><b>5 Stars!!!!!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/c4e9ae96-c0dc-462c-87c5-be0639da10bc_zps61bb6122.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389570363i/8041009.jpg' alt=' photo c4e9ae96-c0dc-462c-87c5-be0639da10bc_zps61bb6122.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>What. A. Ride. Wow! I really loved this book. Stories that are a little on the dark side, maybe even a little disturbing are my favorites! This had the darker elements, but it was also comical, sensual, and beautiful. An intriguing and entertaining read. <br/><br/><br/>The story begins with Sam and Jen. Sam and Jen are injured and on the run. We don’t know why or what happened, all we know is they can never go back. They are no longer Sam and Jen. They are now Lainey and Bree.<br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/402e81d0-89b1-4baf-ab77-3acbdabac455_zps0e8f6ec8.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389608263i/8043546.jpg' alt=' photo 402e81d0-89b1-4baf-ab77-3acbdabac455_zps0e8f6ec8.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Once they get </span>
  <span id="freeText814212953743245845" style="display:none"><b>5 Stars!!!!!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/c4e9ae96-c0dc-462c-87c5-be0639da10bc_zps61bb6122.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389570363i/8041009.jpg" alt=" photo c4e9ae96-c0dc-462c-87c5-be0639da10bc_zps61bb6122.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>What. A. Ride. Wow! I really loved this book. Stories that are a little on the dark side, maybe even a little disturbing are my favorites! This had the darker elements, but it was also comical, sensual, and beautiful. An intriguing and entertaining read. <br><br><br>The story begins with Sam and Jen. Sam and Jen are injured and on the run. We don’t know why or what happened, all we know is they can never go back. They are no longer Sam and Jen. They are now Lainey and Bree.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/402e81d0-89b1-4baf-ab77-3acbdabac455_zps0e8f6ec8.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389608263i/8043546.jpg" alt=" photo 402e81d0-89b1-4baf-ab77-3acbdabac455_zps0e8f6ec8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Once they get far enough away to stop, they end up at a strip club. They decide to go in, clean up and get a drink. That’s all. They end up becoming friends with the clubs owner, Dylan, and get part time jobs waitressing. Bree and Dylan really hit it off. Sam is just happy to be safe, anonymous, and left alone. Then one night, she meets him. Kane. <br><br>Kane is Dylan’s mysterious, dark and strange brother. He is taken by Sam from the moment he lays his eyes on her. This is not normal for him. He does’t get ‘taken’ by anyone. He prefers to stay to himself 99% of the time. He has females he uses, and he see’s his brother every once in a while, but he is the prime definition of the word ‘loner’. Kane has a dark past full of violence. He is an author and I bet you can guess what types of novels he writes. The violence... it’s shaped every part of who he is. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/4cb53378-b755-427c-a340-1da67c7c425f_zpsdcf01753.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389608263i/8043547.jpg" alt=" photo 4cb53378-b755-427c-a340-1da67c7c425f_zpsdcf01753.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Kade Grayson has a plan. To stay as far away from this Lainey as he can. That doesn’t work very well for him. For some reason, she calls to him. He can tell she’s broken, damaged, a mess, just like he is. He wants her but he doesn’t know what to do about it. He’s haunted by his past, he doesn’t want to drag anyone else into it. With her, it could be different. He can tell she has her demons too.<br><i>
  <blockquote>“I think you’re hiding demons too, Samantha Matthews. I want you to introduce me to all of them, because I think I finally found someone whose demons would play nice with my own.”</blockquote>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/4ca185ac-f05b-40e6-b73d-41f6efebc17e_zpsf8d871c4.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389608263i/8043548.jpg" alt=" photo 4ca185ac-f05b-40e6-b73d-41f6efebc17e_zpsf8d871c4.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Kade Kade Kade. I love my broken men. When I first met him, I knew I would love him. He’s mysterious, dangerous, dark and twisted, antisocial and has issues. He can be a straight up asshole. But there was something about him, I just couldn’t get enough. The quote below... that is why I love Kade! :D<br><b>
  <blockquote>Creepy? Yes. Possessive? Absolutely. We all know I have issues. I. Don’t. Care. What. You. Think. </blockquote>
</b> Samantha is a strong heroine. Once you hear her story, wow. She’s feisty, spunky and she had some sense of humor. As dark and serious as this story could be, Sam had me laughing out loud more than once. <br><i>
  <blockquote>“It’s a condom, Kade, because if you’re going to act like a dick, you might as well dress like one,”<br><br>“I’m not surprised, nor could I bring myself to give any fucks about the situation. Seriously, my fucks had been all used up already.” <br><br>“Can your penis reach your rectum? Then go fuck yourself.”<br><br>“You know having a small dick is the leading cause of acting like a big one.” <br><br>“You need a hardcore fucking detox for assholism.”</blockquote>
</i><br><br>As the story continues, Sam and Kane become enamored with one another. They both have dark sides, but they have this connection that cannot be denied. Both having pasts that torment them, they find solace in each other. Sam has never felt the things she feels for Kade before. And the same goes for Kade. He wants to know all of Sam, even her dark side. <br><i>
  <blockquote>“Everything that happened…to me…is stained here,” I whispered, touching my hand to my heart. “It will forever be in my heart, but what I want … is to move it over a little so I can fit you in there too.” </blockquote>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/a0ed12dc-9860-456d-aff3-980a73630106_zps5a913dc1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389608263i/8043549.jpg" alt=" photo a0ed12dc-9860-456d-aff3-980a73630106_zps5a913dc1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <blockquote>I wanted to drown in him. I wanted to feel every inch of that look against my skin. I wanted to touch every last part of him. I wanted to make him call out my name.</blockquote>
</i><br>Two broken people with mysterious and disturbing pasts,end up healing each other, easing some of the pain from the past. But what happens when the past becomes the present? How will these two damaged people cope?<br><br><br><br>Christine Zolendz’s writing is phenomenal. I love the darker reads... they call to me. <i>Brutally Beautiful </i> was captivating, intense, original and completely held my attention. The story was full of suspense and kept me on edge the entire time I was reading. I didn’t want to stop, didn’t want to put it down. An unforgettable read! There was tension, humor, mystery, some crazy hot and sexy scenes, and even some romance. I couldn’t get enough! I’m happy to say there is a second book. And there is no reason to delay reading this, there is NO cliffhanger :D <br><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/f2f86311-1c6f-4f0b-abb5-f444822dd0a3_zpsda6f99eb.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389608263i/8043550.jpg" alt=" photo f2f86311-1c6f-4f0b-abb5-f444822dd0a3_zpsda6f99eb.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“I think the truth is that we are in love with the fantasy of being that one person who could inspire, arouse, or affect someone who is so untouchable to the rest of the world.  It makes us feel special; like we’re the diamond in the rough, the one in a million, the one that everyone else couldn’t be, and do what everyone else couldn’t do.  Imagine being that significant to someone?  To never have to doubt that he loves you, or needs you, or more importantly, wants you more than any other.” </blockquote>
  </b>
</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="814212953743245845" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer799091807" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12577492779234605970"><b>THIS BOOK WAS... <br/>DARK <br/>FUNNY <br/>SEXY<br/>DISTURBING <br/>AND SO BRUTALLY BEAUTIFUL!<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388943374ra/7960877.gif' width='350' height='325' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>CHRISTINE ZOLENDZ EXCEEDED MY EXPECTIONS WITH THIS NOVEL!</b> <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492424499ra/22515116.gif' width='350' height='325' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This story is told in alternate povs (which the author nailed) of a girl named Samantha who is on the run with her bff. She meets a Damaged? Crazy? Stalker? Sexy! HOT! guy named Kade who is crippled emotionally by a traumatic event from his past.<br/><br/><b>
  <i>"Words had always come easily to me. Violence and hate were in my veins. I was rage personified, and horror and malice were </i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText12577492779234605970" style="display:none"><b>THIS BOOK WAS... <br>DARK <br>FUNNY <br>SEXY<br>DISTURBING <br>AND SO BRUTALLY BEAUTIFUL!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388943374ra/7960877.gif" width="350" height="325" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>CHRISTINE ZOLENDZ EXCEEDED MY EXPECTIONS WITH THIS NOVEL!</b> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492424499ra/22515116.gif" width="350" height="325" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This story is told in alternate povs (which the author nailed) of a girl named Samantha who is on the run with her bff. She meets a Damaged? Crazy? Stalker? Sexy! HOT! guy named Kade who is crippled emotionally by a traumatic event from his past.<br><br><b>
  <i>"Words had always come easily to me. Violence and hate were in my veins. I was rage personified, and horror and malice were my only friends. We had lived together peacefully since I came to terms with being me."</i>
</b><br><br>If looking for something different, please give this book a shot. The writing was strong, the characters were fantastic and the story was unforgettable!<br><br><b>
  <i>"No matter how badly it was going to hurt, I didn't want to be anywhere but with Lainey. Let her crush me. Let her destroy me. There wasn't much good left of me, but I wanted her to take every last bit."</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>"I've been broken by lesser men than you, Kade Grayson. Being broken by a good man is something I haven't done. Break me, Kade. Trust in me enough to know you can."</i>
</b><br><br><b>P.S. IT'S NOT PARANORMAL </b><br><br></span>

<div id="review_847299640" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/847299640" />
    <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei"><img alt="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1421992465p2/2551178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/847299640?book_show_action=true">Feb 06, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei">Lady Vigilante (Feifei)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=oops-let-s-do-it-again-romance">oops-let-s-do-it-again-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=douchenugget">douchenugget</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=contemporary-duckie">contemporary-duckie</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=romantic-suspense">romantic-suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=abuse">abuse</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=dee-en-eff">dee-en-eff</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=die-from-cliffhanger">die-from-cliffhanger</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=what-are-you-trying-to-say">what-are-you-trying-to-say</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer847299640" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3077909634355320432"><b>DNF at 73% and stop giving me that look.</b><br/><br/>Yes, I am well aware that this book marks the gazillionith time I did not finish a book since January 2014. So shoot me. I feel it’s justified to give this book a 2 star rating based on what I <i>have</i> read (which let me remind you is nearly 3/4 of the book). Oh and about what I read:<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391805990ra/8459730.gif' width='350' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><u>Some things you should know about me and how I evaluate a book’s worth:</u><br/><br/>1. Heat level and hot sex do not serve as motivation for me to finish a book. Sex is fabulous and in fact I </span>
  <span id="freeText3077909634355320432" style="display:none"><b>DNF at 73% and stop giving me that look.</b><br><br>Yes, I am well aware that this book marks the gazillionith time I did not finish a book since January 2014. So shoot me. I feel it’s justified to give this book a 2 star rating based on what I <i>have</i> read (which let me remind you is nearly 3/4 of the book). Oh and about what I read:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391805990ra/8459730.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>Some things you should know about me and how I evaluate a book’s worth:</u><br><br>1. Heat level and hot sex do not serve as motivation for me to finish a book. Sex is fabulous and in fact I do prefer my books to have steam, but bottom line is I need the story. The plot (and a well-crafted one at that) is what counts. <br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Take the first scene for example. Samantha and Jen are running for their lives, they’re soaked in blood and when they find Dylan’s bar the very next moment they’re flirting with him? You just trivialized whatever ordeal they went through, and not to mention that this part was never ever brought up again until the creepster showed up at 70%. Dylan didn’t even question their identities or whatever happened to them until well after 50%. <b>Unbelievable.</b><br><br>As far as the plot pacing goes...it sucked. The "suspense" part and Samantha running away from her past could've been completely omitted if you asked me. Why? Because it was barely brought up until the 75% mark where Mr. Douche comes looking for her. Throughout the whole book, I kept asking myself "why is she running away?" and "what/who is she running away from?" but it turned out the story is more about Kade than anyone else. And as for the ending! Worst ending in the history of endings. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>2. You write a smart book and I’m immediately a groupie for life. It takes someone extraordinary to win over both my mind and heart so I really don’t expect much here, but at least make your book sound logical instead of having the lust emanate off of the pages. <br><br><b>**I want to say here that if you are a fan of REAL by Katy Evans you will have no problem liking this book, for I found the writing to be eerily similar to that of the “intensity” REAL tried to portray.**</b><br><br>Flowery and fluffy writing to commemorate a particular part of the body? <b>Check.</b><br><br>3. Grammar/Syntax/Writing style. Listen, if I can’t even read your book because of the way it’s styled, <i>then I just can’t read your book.</i> If your story is published, then I expect some quality for what I paid for i.e. little to no grammatical errors and easy-to-follow transitions and above all, <b>mature</b> writing. <br><br>This is one aspect I find necessary to go into extreme detail and fans of this author may beg to differ from my opinion; however it was the main reason why I chose to DNF: <b>horrible writing,</b> to the point where I think my brain was bleeding. Why? BECAUSE SHE WRITES LIKE THIS AND NO IT’S NOT JUST ONE TIME OR A FEW TIMES IT SEEMS LIKE IT’S NECESSARY TO HAVE CAPS IN ALL THE TIME. DID THAT MAKE SENSE I HOPE SO. <br><br><b>
  <i>“Why the hell was I standing here letting him TOUCH ME? WHY the HELL WAS I KISSING HIM BACK?”<br><br>“STOP! A STARBUCKS!”<br><br>“For the first time EVER, I wrote a happy ending. CAN YOU BELIEVE THAT?”<br><br>“HOLY CRAP. I. WAS. SMILING.”<br><br>“WHAT. THE. FUCK.”<br><br>“Why the FUCK was I smiling? This was bad. This had BAD written all the fuck over it.”</i>
</b><br><br>.....<br><br>On top of which, it was painfully obvious that the male POV was written by a female, and an incredibly lackluster POV at that. I can’t count the number of times Kade came off as a whiny, clingy person rather than the brooding, damaged man the author tried to portray him as. The number of “fucks” in the book was also ridiculous, almost as if Kade didn’t say ‘fuck’ every other line I wouldn’t know he’s a guy. <br><br>In hindsight, I should’ve jumped ship at 21% when I <i>knew</i> I wasn’t going to like it, but I tried my best to finish the book until at 73% I didn’t see the story going anywhere. It seems like all I did was just prolong the inevitable: <b>DNF.</b> I will not be reading anymore of this author’s future works. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391806420ra/8459757.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="3077909634355320432" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_801668183" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/801668183" />
    <a title="Patrycja" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6852653-patrycja"><img alt="Patrycja" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1586460589p2/6852653.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/801668183?book_show_action=true">Dec 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patrycja" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patrycja" href="/user/show/6852653-patrycja">Patrycja</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=2014">2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=must-read">must-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer801668183" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer202711399682663813"><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386956402i/7492287._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Title:</b> Brutally Beautiful<br/><b>Series:</b> Brutally Beautiful #1<br/><b>Author:</b> Christine Zolendz<br/><b>Release Date: </b> 5th January, 2014<br/><b>Rating:</b> 4.5 stars<br/><b>Cliffhanger:</b> No. <br/><b> HEA: </b> <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ Yes. The story will be continued, though.  <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386956402i/7492288._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Once again, I was captivated by exceptional storytelling of Zolendz. Only she could came up with a story so bloody and dark and still make it heartbreakingly beautiful. I admire her for that. As much as I loved her previous series, Brutally Beautiful has one advantage more…</span>
  <span id="freeText202711399682663813" style="display:none"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386956402i/7492287._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Title:</b> Brutally Beautiful<br><b>Series:</b> Brutally Beautiful #1<br><b>Author:</b> Christine Zolendz<br><b>Release Date: </b> 5th January, 2014<br><b>Rating:</b> 4.5 stars<br><b>Cliffhanger:</b> No. <br><b> HEA: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Yes. The story will be continued, though.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386956402i/7492288._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Once again, I was captivated by exceptional storytelling of Zolendz. Only she could came up with a story so bloody and dark and still make it heartbreakingly beautiful. I admire her for that. As much as I loved her previous series, Brutally Beautiful has one advantage more… it’s more mature.<br> <br>My mind is still in the story with Sam (Lainey) and Kade. I’m reliving every moment with a big smile on my face, I am still swooning and melting. <br><br>Brutally Beautiful is exceptional and I will have it close to my heart for a very long time. It’s one of those stories that are unforgettable.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389012177i/7970464.png" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The story starts off with a bang. In thrilling way, Zolendz introduce us to main character Samantha. She and her friend are on the run. Both are horribly beaten and are running away from New York and something that happened there. They stop in a strip bar and don’t leave. Both of them get a job as waitress and start a new life. <br><br>2 months of blissful time in the middle of nowhere ends when Kade Grayson steps in the bar. He’s a brother of Dylan, strip club owner. Kade is not normal, though. Horrible past twisted him and inside his head his the beast an reincarnation of the devil himself. He’s a horror novelist. A recluse. He’s damaged. Broken. Twisted. He's the biggest asshole on the whole planet. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"Words had always come easily to me. Violence and hate were in my veins. I was rage personified, and horror and malice were my only friends. We had lived together peacefully since I came to terms with being me."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>And he kind of can’t stop thinking about Lainey. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"No matter how badly it was going to hurt, I didn't want to be anywhere but with Lainey. Let her crush me. Let her destroy me. There wasn't much good left of me, but I wanted her to take every last bit." </blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389012177i/7970465.png" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What can I say? Christine Zolendz took me on amazingly agonizing journey. Journey filled with hope, small light in the darkness and brutally beautiful love that blossoms there. I was amazed. Dazed. Thrilled. I was left completely breathless. I loved almost every sentence. This book was like no other I have ever read. So complex and unique it took my breath away!<br><br>I loved everything. And I really mean it. Not only the plot was fast paced, refreshing and mesmerizing. Zolendz characters were complex, beautiful and well thought. Every aspect of their personalities was realistic. And Kade… This man was so sexy that I still tremble when I think of him.<br><br>Together Sam and Kade were amazing. I ached for them. I cried with them. I wanted to pray for the bad to go away and leave them alone. I never felt so related to the couple I've read about. They made it so easy to love them and hurt for them. My skin is still buzzing with this feelings. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389012177i/7970467.png" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Overall, Brutally Beautiful was funny, sexy, heartbreaking and stunning story. I enjoyed it immensely and I can’t wait for more. My only issue was the rushed ending, that didn’t exactly satisfy me, but I know next part of the series will make it perfect. <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386956727i/7492465._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="202711399682663813" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2283314506?book_show_action=true">Feb 05, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2283314506" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15868638914420686785"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1517850506i/25007743._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This is the first book in the BEAUTIFUL duet. It doesn’t end in a cliffhanger; it ends in a HFN but there are still secrets unrevealed, so we need book 2 for the story to come to full circle. <br/><br/>***********************************************<br/><br/>Normally, I'd wait and write my review after I finish reading the series but I need to talk about this book asap. I loved it. It was like a breath of fresh air with its exquisite writing.<br/><br/>Ms Zolendz does it again and creates a one hell of a story and we are intr</span>
  <span id="freeText15868638914420686785" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1517850506i/25007743._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is the first book in the BEAUTIFUL duet. It doesn’t end in a cliffhanger; it ends in a HFN but there are still secrets unrevealed, so we need book 2 for the story to come to full circle. <br><br>***********************************************<br><br>Normally, I'd wait and write my review after I finish reading the series but I need to talk about this book asap. I loved it. It was like a breath of fresh air with its exquisite writing.<br><br>Ms Zolendz does it again and creates a one hell of a story and we are introduced to the tormented world of two damaged people.<br><br>***********************************************<br><br><b>This is a brutally beautiful book. </b><br><br><i>There is darkness in it. </i><br>Abuse. <br>Violence. <br>Massacre. <br>Murder.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/558534.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>And there is also light in it. </i><br>Love. <br>Lust. <br>Hope. <br>Healing. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1517850847i/25007762._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It is written bloody well and my book is full of highlights.<br><br>***********************************************<br><br>You need to read the <b>Author’s Note</b> before starting the book. <br><br>Ms Zolendz warns us there that in real life, not every story is pretty or perfect, and she emphasizes that Samantha and Kade’s story is also full of ugly and painful happenings but still it has its own beauty - as I said, their story is brutally beautiful. <br><br>What these two people have experienced are quite like the horror stories that we watch on the news and this awesome book is dedicated to victims of violence and abuse. <br><br>Like the writer, I also wish them to find peace and calmness in their life.<br><br>***********************************************<br><br><b>The beginning:</b><br><br>The book begins with Samantha and her best friend Jennifer driving crazy fast, away from a bloody scene. They drive for 7 hours and end up in a town in the Adirondack Mountains, where they find a shelter and work to do. <br><br>They now go by the names of Lainey &amp; Bree.<br><br>Jennifer (Bree) is attracted to Dylan, the owner of the bar where they work and Samantha (Lainey) soon meets and is strongly drawn to Dylan's brother Kade, who is a wild man, tormented and haunted by his past. <br><br>***********************************************<br><br><b>The mystery called "Kade":</b><br><br>Kade is living a life of solitude, hiding himself from the entire outside world and fighting with his PTSD on his own. His inner demons and his traumatized mind has surprisingly caused him to become a very famous and successful writer of horror books. <br><br>Kade only interacts with people when it is very necessary. To the people around him, he looks intimidating, arrogant and dangerous. He doesn’t care what other people think, though, he just lets them think he is a monster.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1517850506i/25007745._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Kade's obsession with Samantha:</b><br><br>When Kade sees Samantha in the bar where she works as a waitress, he instantly becomes fascinated by her. She is not your classical beauty but she is stunning in her own way, which captivates him at the first look. <br><br>The way she walks, the way she talks to people and her smart mind all fascinate him but at first, he doesn’t want to believe she is real. He has serious trust issues. He believes she is also not to be trusted like all other human beings. He thinks she is faking this perfect personality. That’s why, first he treats her in a demeaning way to test her and I was really pissed at him then but Samantha is one of the most awesome heroines ever - a smartas*, a real kickas*! Her witty comebacks and her self-respect soon make Kade realize that she is real and not pretending and with every new thing he discovers about her, he sees that she is perfection. <br><br>When Kade believes in Samantha and starts to trust her, he becomes even more obsessed with her. Although normally he comes to town 3 or 4 times a year, he starts to come to the bar she is working (and his brother owns) more often now, just to watch her.<br><br>***********************************************<br><br><b>Safety: </b><br><br>I must warn you that Kade is unlikable at first. He even has sex with another woman (a married one) before he starts something with Samantha (so this book may not be safe for every reader.) <br><br>On the other hand, before Samantha and Kade become a couple, Samantha goes out with a man called Francis a few times but they only kiss and do not go further than that.<br><br>Obviously, nothing about this book says it is hearts and flowers. It is not a happy sappy light and fun romance. This is the love story of two very scarred souls who do not intend to fall in love with anyone so their falling in love doesn't happen as smoothly as readers with romantic hearts might expect. <br><br>But when it happens, when they let themselves fall for each other, then, it is worth all the pain!<br><br>***********************************************<br><br><b>The unavoidable attraction grows!</b><br><br>The more Samantha and Kade interact with each other, the more they understand they have something in common: "their traumatized past &amp; the violence they had to endure." <br><br>They are both scarred souls. This draws them to one another even more strongly. However, full trust is not earned easily, especially if the person has been abused before because they trusted easily. Therefore, their revealing their darkest secrets to one another take time.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1517850506i/25007748._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>At one point, it becomes impossible for Samantha and Kade to resist the powerful chemistry between them. They are slowly but forcefully drawn to one another with an undeniable attraction, which gradually grows into a powerful story of love and redemption.<br><br>***********************************************<br><br><b>Resolution</b>:<br><br>Their story doesn’t have a full resolution in this book, it has a HFN ending. When the book ends, some secrets are still buried deep and I guess they will haunt them in Book 2 :(<br><br>Now, before I begin to read Book 2, I want to say that this book is worth reading because of the story it tells and because of the amazing way it is told by the talented story-teller / writer C. Zolendz. <br><br>It is written in dual point of view. The way Ms Zolendz uses her magic word engraves everything into your heart, every feeling is etched into your soul and she is damn good about creating unique characters with unique stories to tell.<br><br>If you ask me, this book is definitely one that you need to put in your “must-read” shelf if you can read books that are a little on the dark side.<br><br>***********************************************<br><br><b>QUOTES from the book:</b><br><br>Let me leave you with the perfection of some quotes from the book that may help you to decide if you want to give this book a chance…<br><br><b>
  <i>Life as I knew it was over. <br>My life. <br>Over. <br>That woman I once was, Samantha Matthews, was gone. <br>Left for dead. <br>Everything and everyone I ever knew…<br>Everything I had ever worked for… gone. <br>Just. Like. That. <br>Poof. <br>Gone.<br><br>***<br><br>I didn’t cry from fear, or hurt, or pain. <br>I cried for Samantha Matthews, the woman that they forced me not to be. <br>For everything I lost. <br><br>There are only a few words I have left in my mind for them: <br>You never should have underestimated me. <br><br>***<br><br>I’ve felt love and lust before. But this, what I felt while this dangerous man fucked me vigorously with his eyes, it was insane. Intense… </i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1517850506i/25007747._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>I learned an invaluable lesson once. If I stayed silent for long enough, and just watched long enough, people and life would pass by me, as if I were invisible. Or dead.<br><br>***<br><br>I had no idea what I had just witnessed, but that little-bit-of-a-wisp waitress seemed to have put that wanker in his place with her presence and words. <br>Unafraid and confident. <br>Fearless. <br>Impressive and deadly sexy. <br>Beyond sexy. <br>That was the sexiest thing I’d ever witnessed outside of porn.<br><br>***<br><br>The plain raw intelligence of her face was utterly breathtaking and for the first time in my life, I couldn’t find the correct adjectives to describe something. No mere words would have done her natural beauty justice or could have described the way she moved. </i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1517850506i/25007746._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>It was like… liquid. <br>That’s the only word I had for her. <br>Flowing, fluid, melting into everything with a precision that seemed naturally calculated. <br><br>I felt like Adam looking at Eve for the first time, having never seen another woman before her.<br><br>***<br><br>He’s tainted with a ton of issues. He’s a loner anyway, doesn’t date, and doesn’t enjoy being around people. He’s pretty savage.<br><br>***<br><br>“Fuck. Are your eyes green?” <br>“Yes. Scandalous isn’t it? Maybe I should poke them out for you and insert a color of your choice? Are you against all green-eyed waitresses taking your orders, or am I the only lucky one?” <br><br>***<br><br>“Your intimidation skills are lacking and I’m not the kind of woman who would actually believe that you are superior to me just because you’re a man. You think you’re better than me and you’re not Kade.<br>…<br>If I’m not good enough because I’m a waitress, don't settle for me, don't sink down to my level. You don't deserve anything I have to offer. Let that shit hurt for a hot minute, simmer in it then leave me the fuck alone. <br><br>Repeat that shit to yourself in your head when you walk out of here, rinse and repeat.”<br><br>***<br><br>“You know what they say, having a small dick is the leading cause of acting like a big one.”<br><br>***<br><br>“You’re adorable when you’re angry,” he whispered, breathing heavily. <br>“Oh, really? Then get the hell off me, because I’m about to get gorgeous all over your ass.”<br><br>***<br><br>Lainey. <br>Lainey. <br>Lainey. <br>I could barely see straight as I staggered into my office. <br>I had to shake this need, this desire to know her. <br>I felt cursed. <br>Possessed. <br>Her face haunted me. <br>Her laughter echoed in my brain. <br>Her smile plagued my thoughts. <br><br>But mostly it was her calmness that affected me. <br>Soothed me. <br>Mollified the rage. <br><br>Who was she really? <br>Where did she come from? <br>What happened that she ended up bloody beaten at my brother’s bar?</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1517850506ra/25007742.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>I was a thirty-two-year old woman and I’d never been kissed like this before. <br>Ever. <br><br>Kade Grayson kissed the thoughts right out of my head, kissed my fears and anxiousness away, leaving me empty, and then poured himself in. </i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469155546ra/19786542.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>“You make me smile when your lips are on mine, like I’m borrowing your happiness, like it’s wiping off on me. Maybe I’m just stealing it, I don’t know. <br><br>All I know is that it gives me a calmness, a happiness I never thought I could feel…you give me a reason…"<br><br>***<br><br>"She was mine, and no other’s. Only my lips could kiss hers. Only my hands could hold hers. Only my body could sink deep inside her between those smooth ivory thighs…<br><br>And only she could tame the beast I was. Only she could quench the thirst I hungered after, and coax the monster inside me to be a man again, if only a broken one…”<br><br>***<br><br> “I think you’re hiding demons too, Samantha Matthews. I want you to introduce me to all of them, because I think I finally found someone whose demons would play nice with my own.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1517850506ra/25007741.gif" width="420" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>“I want to see all of you, Sam. Every scar.” <br><br>Leaning forward, his elbows pressed into his knees, his whispers tickled my ears, “Then I’m going to make you forget how you got each fucking one.”<br><br>***<br><br>“Cliffhanger almost killed me. How does it end,” I whispered against his lips. <br>“Comes out next month,” he said, as warm lips brushed past mine. <br>“How does it end?” <br>“Brutally beautiful.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1517850506i/25007744._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_801490908" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/801490908" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/801490908?book_show_action=true">Dec 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer801490908" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6749385554342828802"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389416858i/8029512._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389126887i/7992812._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>*** FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED *** 4.5 stars!! <br/><br/>Fast-paced, witty and intriguing, <em>Brutally Beautiful</em> was a dark and yet delightfully gripping book that hooked me from the start and kept me flipping pages long into the night. It was SO well-written. The dialogue was snappy, the plot was kept me on my toes, and the story was raw and emotionally intense. This book was truly a joy to read and I have quotes highlighted on almost every single page. If you are a fan of dark, tortured heroes and strong heroi</span>
  <span id="freeText6749385554342828802" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389416858i/8029512._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389126887i/7992812._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>*** FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED *** 4.5 stars!! <br><br>Fast-paced, witty and intriguing, <em>Brutally Beautiful</em> was a dark and yet delightfully gripping book that hooked me from the start and kept me flipping pages long into the night. It was SO well-written. The dialogue was snappy, the plot was kept me on my toes, and the story was raw and emotionally intense. This book was truly a joy to read and I have quotes highlighted on almost every single page. If you are a fan of dark, tortured heroes and strong heroines, you should definitely add this book to your reading list. <br><br>The dedication at the beginning already had my heart clenching...<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"Dedicated to the ones that are bruised and broken."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>... and with an opening line like the following, this book instantly grabbed my attention!<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"There was blood all over my hands and I knew I was losing control, because I was more desperate to find a drink, than a napkin to clean off the mess."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>The story starts off with the heroine, Sam, escaping her violent, pain-filled life literally with blood still on her hands and running deep into the mountains with her best friend which is where she meets Kade -- a man hiding a dark past and even more secrets than her.... I don't really want to say more though. That is the main set up of the story but the rest of the details are all a journey I suggest you just dive into :)<br><br>I adored the hero, Kade!!! He was such a complex and intuguing character. He was a complete mystery to me -- almost an anti-hero honestly. He was dark (and I mean DARKKKKKK), an antisocial, Alpha loner with a world of issues and a mysterious past. He was antagonistic and intense, at times he felt dangerous but I knew he was just damaged, he could be a total jerk one minute but then turn around the next moment and say or do something that made my heart just melt. He was far from perfect but I totally loved him!!<br><br>Actually, if you're a fan of Matt Sky (the hero of Night Owl), you'll probably love Kade because in many ways he and Matt felt like long lost brothers!<br><br>I'll totally admit though -- he did not make it easy to love him at first. I was totally drawn to his character when I first "met" him and was already starting to like him but then, he opened his mouth.<br><br>WHAT.<br>AN.<br>ASSHOLE.<br><br>I mean really. But... the more I learned about him, the more I realized that while he had issues, he was a really good guy at heart and hiding behind the antagonistic facade he wore was a broken man haunted by the demons of his brutal past.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"Violence and hate were in my veins. I was rage personified, and horror and malicee were my friends. We had lived together peacefully since I came to terms with being me."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>The heroine was just awesome! She'd been through hell but she held her head high and was NOT the kind of woman to let a man walk over her. She was funny, sassy, and strong and I just loved her for it!<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"I'm sure Kade Grayson had a long line of interested women offering their dancing services to him for his money, but I wasn't going to be one of them."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>The story was told in alternating POVs. I loved getting both sides of the story and, because I liked both Sam and Kade, I loved seeing the story through their eyes. Kade's POV though was especially interesting. It was fascinating, dark, funny, totally weird and yet surprisingly normal, a touch disturbing at times but also just pure awesome!! Like I said, that man was DARK -- his thoughts and actions were borderline unhinged at times...<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"I wanted to hate her, break her, and keep her the hell away from my sick, twisted mind. But, there was no point in lying to myself, was there? Because I wanted a taste of her even more. I wanted her."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>But I loved how Sam was the first person to be able to break through his walls and get to the real HIM. Still, it was a love, hate, love, hate, love, hate type relationship filled with amazing banter, a healthy dose of eye fucking and sexual tension out the wazoo!<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"We were a mere inches away from each other, and ready to either claw each other's eyes out or lick each other silly."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>Kade just kept on surprising me but I loved how this dark and twisted man was getting completely unravelled by this girl who wouldn't take any of his shit and who he couldn't keep off his mind.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"Yeah, I was going to follow her. Staying away from her was not an option…. Fran dropped her off at a grocery store. Psycho me followed her in."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>So yeah, he was an asshole, a jerk, a wee bit of a stalker, and certainly seemed more than a little crazy BUT I LOVED HIM!!! I couldn't not. He was a man haunted by the nightmares of his past but something about Sam helped to heal him... slowly.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"You somehow soothe the chaos that's inside me. You heal me."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>Now with the way it's written, there's SO much that's hidden and mysterious and honestly, there were times when some of the content got so dark that a part of me almost wondered if the story was maybe a paranormal one but... no - it's fully contemporary, real life. And, it all makes sense in the end!<br><br>But my mind was racing -- what could possibly have happened to make Kade the way he was? "<em>What could possibly make a grown man choose a reclusive existence and have such a strong distaste for other human beings?"</em> .... Well, I won't tell you what it is but the answer was HEART BREAKING!! It also explained everything. It made me desperately wish I could hug him but most of all it made me genuinely understand him. All of a sudden all of his "strange" behaviour and actions made sense.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"People who have seen real life monsters up close will never feel understood by people who haven't. What those people don't understand, is that we still see those monsters, everyday."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>I really love seeing strong heroines such as Sam. While Kade was absolutely an Alpha, <em>she </em>was the one who saved him and I absolutely love that.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"Everything that happened… to me… is stained here," I whisper, touching my hand to my heart. "It will forever be in my heart, but what I want, Sam is to move it over a little so I can fit you in there too."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>Guys, I need to say this again -- the WRITING was <em>awesome</em>!!!! Smart, snappy, <em>intelligent -- </em>it kept me highlighting like crazy. It was brilliant. I was right <em>there</em> in the story. The style was so real - very direct and so visually rich. With a great balance between darkness and humor. I had a very hard time choosing only a few quotes to include with this review. For example, I loved the banter...<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"It's too early to laugh," I mumbled...</em>
    <br>
    <br>
    <em> "Why? Do you hate morning people?" she asked, smiling.</em>
    <br>
    <br>
    <em> "It has nothing to do with morning… it's the people part." I retorted…</em>
    <br>
    <br>
    <em> "Mr. Grayson, your charm is showing. You might want to tuck it back in."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>I loved the humor...<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"Coitus Interruptus!" I screamed. "Stop and put your hands where I can see them."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>I loved the descriptions...<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"This was bad. This had BAD written all the fuck over it. This… this is just a morbid filled ice cream cone dipped in psycho flavoured sprinkles."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>And I loved the randomest lines that just made me smile...<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"I've been to his place; he lives in harmony with his dust bunnies."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>Ok now the ending got intense!! Ohhhh my gosh there was a scene that had my heart in my THROAT!!!! Worst nightmare!! And, while it did feel a touch over-dramatic, I was really grateful to have all my questions in full detail. <br><br>I'm happy to say that there is no cliffhanger at the end. If you wanted, you <em>could</em> in fact read this as a standalone novel but there is an optional teaser chapter at the end that leaves you wanting more. Luckily, the next book will be out in a few weeks so you won't have long to wait if you're wanting more from these characters. <br><br>Overall, this was really a wonderful read! Fantastic writing, <em>great </em>characters, and a fast-paced, gripping story that I could not put down. I loved it and would definitely recommend adding it to your reading lists!!<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"It was beautiful and dark, twisted and profound." </blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>4.5 stars.<br><br>CASTING: See above<br><br>****************************<br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>

</a><br/><br/><b>
  <i> "Something dark haunts us all. What darkness haunts you at night? What do you squeeze your eyes closed to when the darkness bites against your back when you're alone at night? Because I was married to mine. I was daughter to mine, and I refused to look in the mirror and see it make me as dark as them, so I walked away from it all."<br/></i>
</b><br/><br/>They are battered, broken and bloody and wind up at a strip bar in the m</span>
  <span id="freeText11678373775396507028" style="display:none"><b>4.5 This shit is crazy stars....</b><br><br>Samantha Matthews and best friend Jen are on the run. <br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%202/tumblr_inline_myhmqjuqLh1rejlqe_zpse0dc445b.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389058159ra/7980238.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_inline_myhmqjuqLh1rejlqe_zpse0dc445b.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i> "Something dark haunts us all. What darkness haunts you at night? What do you squeeze your eyes closed to when the darkness bites against your back when you're alone at night? Because I was married to mine. I was daughter to mine, and I refused to look in the mirror and see it make me as dark as them, so I walked away from it all."<br></i>
</b><br><br>They are battered, broken and bloody and wind up at a strip bar in the middle of BFE. They become Lainey and Bree as their cover.There they meet bar owner, Dylan, and talk him into giving them both jobs.<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY/tumblr_m67eyrRqbC1qf45lpo1_400_zps62fc77c5.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389060837ra/7980815.gif" alt="hallelujar photo tumblr_m67eyrRqbC1qf45lpo1_400_zps62fc77c5.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Dylan's brother, Kade, happens to come by the bar and is immediately attracted to Lainey (Samantha) when he sees her confrontation with a drunk bar patron.<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY/tumblr_mf3bq9PBpx1rcny7ko1_500_zps4d59fb50.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389060073ra/7980573.gif" alt="die photo tumblr_mf3bq9PBpx1rcny7ko1_500_zps4d59fb50.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Kade is some kind of fucked up...Yeah, he's got some issues.....Girls always wind up attracted to the ones with some problems though....And he's hot so of course that helps. <br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY/messeduphead_zpsa425c14e.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389060073ra/7980574.gif" alt="crazy photo messeduphead_zpsa425c14e.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>He had a traumatic experience as a child and is haunted by it every day. This has led him to be a successful writer but he is constantly battling his demons and somewhat of a hermit.<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%202/ckkSAdu_zps7898e3cd.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389058159ra/7980240.gif" alt="feels photo ckkSAdu_zps7898e3cd.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>For some reason Lainey goes on a few dates with hippie weirdo, Fran aka Francis<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%202/8ec55cec-0f8f-462a-a3c3-d1084163c83a_zps7d07ef54.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389060186i/7980598._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 8ec55cec-0f8f-462a-a3c3-d1084163c83a_zps7d07ef54.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Francis wants to be with her but she doesn't want a relationship. He is absolutely no competition for Kade, he just gets in the way a little bit.<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY/tumblr_lz5u16Ly4C1qfwumo_zpsf4f98fc9.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389060531ra/7980756.gif" alt="GET OUT photo tumblr_lz5u16Ly4C1qfwumo_zpsf4f98fc9.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Lainey and Kade have some <b>MAJOR</b> sexual tension. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/502032.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I love the way she is a smart ass and challenges him constantly<br><br><b>
  <i>"You’re acting like a bitch, and if I wanted a bitch, I would have adopted a dog."<br><br>"I pity you for defining yourself because of the four walls you box yourself into." </i>
</b><br><br>Kade tries to stay away but its impossible<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389060837ra/7980816.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"Like a wrecking ball, she came in, crumbling my walls into dust… She was as broken as I was…I could see some sort of pain in those green depths, some sort of mirrored knowledge that the world sucked. And, I thought to myself…finally…finally someone on my side of the fishbowl. I wanted to know what haunted her and hold hands in the darkness…together…"</i>
</b><br><br>Sorry but this was the first thing that came to my mind....HAHAHAHA!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389060531ra/7980757.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And they are just hot together...<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%202/tumblr_m9nfj3mf0L1qahhfpo1_500_zps7117462b.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389058159ra/7980242.gif" alt="toast photo tumblr_m9nfj3mf0L1qahhfpo1_500_zps7117462b.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But the question is will they heal each other or will their pasts catch up to them and they remain broken?<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%202/NPH-SHRUG_zpsb389e23e.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389059370ra/7980491.gif" alt="shrug photo NPH-SHRUG_zpsb389e23e.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I loved Christine's writing. Lainey was a very relatable character in my opinion. Also we share the Starbucks love. :)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389058159i/7980243.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I will say the only thing about this book is another book with fucking grey eyes....I mean really!!<br><br>Anyways, should you read this book?<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY/tumblr_mjl4zaQhnO1s7tuayo1_r2_500_zps9f2cbd31.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380387684ra/747820.gif" alt="absolutely photo tumblr_mjl4zaQhnO1s7tuayo1_r2_500_zps9f2cbd31.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

    <a title="Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13273769-farah-professor-dean-s-beauty"><img alt="Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1481371426p2/13273769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/822163200?book_show_action=true">Jan 13, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*" href="/user/show/13273769-farah-professor-dean-s-beauty">Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer822163200" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5075313115296456541"><br/><br/><br/>Wow!   <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7500821-vishous?shelf=hot-hot-guyzzz">hot-hot-guyzzz</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7500821-vishous?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7500821-vishous?shelf=review">review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7500821-vishous?shelf=need-sequel-pronto">need-sequel-pronto</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer801529725" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6881803293840002651">Ok, around the first half of the book I seriously loved it! Loved it so much that I thought nothing could make me not love it so much later. <br/>The writing was amazing, I swear I highlighted almost the whole book. There wasn't one thing I didn't love with the writing. And with the story. I loved it all. I loved all the characters. So what made me give it 4 stars? I would have given it 3.5 but I round it up to 4. <br/><br/>Him. His mood swings. In the beginning he was amazing, he was so dark and twisted and I</span>
  <span id="freeText6881803293840002651" style="display:none">Ok, around the first half of the book I seriously loved it! Loved it so much that I thought nothing could make me not love it so much later. <br />The writing was amazing, I swear I highlighted almost the whole book. There wasn't one thing I didn't love with the writing. And with the story. I loved it all. I loved all the characters. So what made me give it 4 stars? I would have given it 3.5 but I round it up to 4. <br /><br />Him. His mood swings. In the beginning he was amazing, he was so dark and twisted and I was mesmerized with his mind and all of his thoughts. He was an asshole and I loved that. He was an asshole pretty much all the time, even when he was trying to be good to her. But later on, his constant mood swings, which were literally up and down, hot and cold, without any normal progression from any state of mind to other were giving me a slight headache in the end. There wasn't any scale how his emotions escalated, they were, literally, seriously manic. Don't get me wrong, his character is like some maniac, but one sentence all peachy and then next sentence he is yelling and growling or whatever, for no reason. <br /><br />The story was great, and it can be read as stand-alone, which I thought it was when I started reading it. It has an HEA, but after finishing it, and seeing there is a teaser for the next book which had a fu@king cliff-hanger, I was wondering why would you do that? Why would you finish a book and then give like the first chapter of next in the end with a cliff?!?! Why then not finish a book with a cliff?!?!?! Or simply not give a peek into next one?!?!<br /><br />Both of them hiding something, she is running and living in fear will she be found, and he simply embracing his dark side and not being social, but writing all his thoughts in his books, all his violent thoughts that made him who he is in one event in the past was really a great thing to read. <br /><br />He, as a writer... Simply stunning...<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>"Dealing with thoughts about her would end up like all my thoughts did, in sickening violence. I would need to find more words to match her beauty and somehow mar her fictional existence in my head with the exquisite release of her last breath, or possess her with demons, slaughter her by the hands of a delusional lover, disfigure her in a gruesome accident or something equally horrifying"<br /><br />"My muse would not shut the fuck up. The obsession consumed me for days. The girl, I knew would be an obsession for longer. I wanted to scrape the words I’ve written off the white of the screen, grab them tightly in my hand and smash them against her face. Have her feel my words against her flesh, smear them into her pores, and have them seep into her skin"</i>
</blockquote><br /><br />With her, you have no idea who she really is until near the end. You know something happened, but who she really is... I didn't see it coming and I actually loved it a lot. She did get on my nerves when she gave him that poetic talk in his car, but in general I liked her because she was a strong character and not some whiny woman. <br /><br />And now all that's left is waiting for the story to continue and see how ill it be fu@ked up. It was too good to be true, and the thought of actual teaser was somewhere in the back of my mind, but I was hoping for normal stand-alone.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6881803293840002651" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
