<div id="review_1765568352" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1765568352" />
    <a title="Natalie ✩★ The Biblioholic ★✩" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/39243185-natalie-the-biblioholic"><img alt="Natalie ✩★ The Biblioholic ★✩" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1529028941p2/39243185.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1765568352?book_show_action=true">Sep 23, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Natalie ✩★ The Biblioholic ★✩" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Natalie ✩★ The Biblioholic ★✩" href="/user/show/39243185-natalie-the-biblioholic">Natalie ✩★ The Biblioholic ★✩</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39243185-natalie-the-biblioholic?shelf=suspense">suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39243185-natalie-the-biblioholic?shelf=abusive-past">abusive-past</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39243185-natalie-the-biblioholic?shelf=sexy-times">sexy-times</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39243185-natalie-the-biblioholic?shelf=dark">dark</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39243185-natalie-the-biblioholic?shelf=dual-pov">dual-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39243185-natalie-the-biblioholic?shelf=medical">medical</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39243185-natalie-the-biblioholic?shelf=writer">writer</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1765568352" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8877510659479312254">Whoa! Whoa Whoa Whoa Whoa Whoa Whoa Whoa!!<br/><br/>This story was jam-packed with so many feels and I'm not talking the warm and fuzzy kind. Christine Zolendz did an incredible job of blending drama, family, friendship, chemistry, eroticism, pain, despair and trauma. She did all that and still found a way to inject a lot of humour along the way.<br/><br/>Samantha was a brilliant and renowned head trauma surgeon, but she was running away from her life. She was escaping a life filled with lies and was hoping to outr</span>
  <span id="freeText8877510659479312254" style="display:none">Whoa! Whoa Whoa Whoa Whoa Whoa Whoa Whoa!!<br><br>This story was jam-packed with so many feels and I'm not talking the warm and fuzzy kind. Christine Zolendz did an incredible job of blending drama, family, friendship, chemistry, eroticism, pain, despair and trauma. She did all that and still found a way to inject a lot of humour along the way.<br><br>Samantha was a brilliant and renowned head trauma surgeon, but she was running away from her life. She was escaping a life filled with lies and was hoping to outrun and overcome her demons. My impressions of Sam were that she was strong, beautiful (inside and out), loving, generous, compassionate, intelligent, witty, and a freaking survivor with balls of steel.<br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474675852i/20631034.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br>Kade was equally damaged. He survived an extremely traumatic event in his youth and hasn't been the same since. He's lost all of his joy in life. He has cut himself off from society, isolating himself with his darkness. His pain has sparked a successful career as an author of horror. I for one loved getting the chance to explore Kade's mind through his POV. It was dark and twisted, as I expected, but I adored the way he viewed every thing. I especially loved how obsessive he became for Sam. LOVED IT!!<br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474676338i/20631065.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br>That quote right there... ^^^^^^^... That's Sam and Kade.<br><br>I enjoyed the banter these two shared. It had a life of its own. Tennis or Ping Pong-worthy banter. The humour gave some relief to the depth of the story, a bit of light in such a dark tunnel. Otherwise it really would have been too depressing for our broken (or not so broken?) heroes and <b>
  <u>no one</u>
</b> wants that. I'm sure <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20272153.Cold_Blooded_Beautiful__Beautiful___2_" title="Cold-Blooded Beautiful (Beautiful, #2) by Christine Zolendz" rel="nofollow noopener">Cold-Blooded Beautiful</a> will deal with Samantha's monster aka David and I cannot wait to bear witness to his destruction.<br><br>I recommend this book to any and all who love their books intense, dark, sexy and suspenseful!</span>
  <a data-text-id="8877510659479312254" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText5044124863266447711" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>”I learned an invaluable lesson once. If I stayed silent for long enough, and just watched long enough, people and life would pass by me, as if I were invisible. Or dead. </blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>I was excited to start this story because all of my friends have loved this book, so far. I was told it was dark and twisted. I spent most of the book waiting for it to get dark and twisted. By the time it started to become that way towards the end I was not really feeling it. I really love dark books and had high hopes for this one. <br><br>After I was half way through I mentioned to a friend that I’m not sure why I’m not connecting with this book and that I'm not sure if it's me or the book. Her answer,<b> “It’s you.”</b> I laughed so hard because she was so honest with me. <span id="freeTextContainer18242068257373759497"><b>DNF @ Page 57</b><br/><br/><b>SAFE GANG: WARNING! EXPLICIT SEX SCENES WITH OW</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s875.photobucket.com/user/jakubowsa/media/tumblr_m3wy7ajyJg1qbgi86o1_500_zpsavtqk1h7.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/>As soon as the Hero took the OW out and screwed her in his car meaning after he already met the heroine and obsessed about her I was done with him! <br/><br/><b>"I don't read a romance for those scenes, I read a romance for the celebration of love and how the best love helps us to grow..."Those sex scenes with OW" are not the portrayal of the best love I want to feel in my romance book"</b><br/><br/>This is my second book by this author and the last!         <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer826757648" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer14452092866347311046"><b> 5 Stars <i>(Originally Read 1/17/2014)</i></b><br/><br/><b> 3.5 Stars <i>(Re-Read 5/29/2019)</i></b><br/><br/><b>Overall Opinion: </b>I just finished the book <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20454672.Mean_Streak' title='Mean Streak by Sandra Brown' rel='nofollow noopener'>Mean Streak</a> and parts of it reminded me of this book, so when I realized I never wrote a review for it -- I jumped right in for a re-read. I'm bummed to say that this will be taken off my favorites shelf and my rating will be going down. I found myself feeling conflicted about the characters where I wanted just a little more back story, especially with the h, because I struggled with conne</span>
  <span id="freeText14452092866347311046" style="display:none"><b> 5 Stars <i>(Originally Read 1/17/2014)</i></b><br /><br /><b> 3.5 Stars <i>(Re-Read 5/29/2019)</i></b><br /><br /><b>Overall Opinion: </b>I just finished the book <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20454672.Mean_Streak" title="Mean Streak by Sandra Brown" rel="nofollow noopener">Mean Streak</a> and parts of it reminded me of this book, so when I realized I never wrote a review for it -- I jumped right in for a re-read. I'm bummed to say that this will be taken off my favorites shelf and my rating will be going down. I found myself feeling conflicted about the characters where I wanted just a little more back story, especially with the h, because I struggled with connecting to them. I don't doubt that I loved this when I read it the first time because it's definitely unique in the characters' life experiences -- but, I just felt like there were too many unanswered questions and moments where I was scratching my head in questioning what was happening. I know that these questions very well could be answered in the next book, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20272153.Cold_Blooded_Beautiful__Beautiful___2_" title="Cold-Blooded Beautiful (Beautiful, #2) by Christine Zolendz" rel="nofollow noopener">Cold-Blooded Beautiful</a>, but honestly I feel kind of meh about continuing. I might just skim it to see what happens, but overall this was a little bit better than "just okay" 3 Stars for me.<br /><br /><b>Brief Summary of the Storyline: </b> This is Samantha and Kade's story. Samantha and her best friend show up in a small town bar beaten up and end up staying and changing their identities. Samantha meets the mysterious and extremely rude brother, Kade, of her new boss and can't help but be oddly drawn to him. Kade comes with his own heavy baggage but he cannot get Samantha out of his head. There are some big secrets revealed, some sexy times, and some suspenseful moments...and they get a HFN ending.<br /><br /><b>POV:</b> This alternated between Samantha and Kade's POV.<br /><br /><b>Overall Pace of Story: </b> Good. I never skimmed and I thought it flowed well.<br /><br /><b>Instalove:</b> No. Instalust? Yes.<br /><br /><b>H rating:</b> 3 stars. Kade. He was a mess! Understandably so, IMO, because of his past. I appreciated how he worked through some of his personal demons for the h.<br /><br /><b>h rating:</b> 3 stars. Samantha. I appreciated her strength and how she always kept calm for others, but I absolutely wanted more depth in her background.<br /><br /><b>Sadness level: </b>Low, no tissues needed<br /><br /><b>Push/Pull:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[They both push away and also pursue the relationship at times.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Heat level:</b> Hot. They have some hot tension, chemistry, and scenes -- but not so much it takes away from the story. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Some light bdsm qualities like spanking, bondage, and D/s talk. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Descriptive sex:</b> Yes<br /><br /><b>OW/OM drama:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The h is on the run from her abusive husband. The h is also being pursued by OM (that she kisses).  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Sex scene with OW or OM:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[There is a scene where the H is with his f-buddy (that married to OM), and another scene with him kicking a different OW (ONS) out of his house. These scenes happen before anything substantial happens between the h and H.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Cheating: </b> Yes technically <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The h is technically married to OM that she is on the run from when she meets the H and is intimate with him.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Separation:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[They are separated physically (but not in the relationship sense) for ~2 months, but there was no mention or suggestion of other partners during this time.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Possible Triggers: </b>Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Domestic violence/school shooting/suicide of friend (off page), violence/attempted murder (on page), and the H has PTSD (on page)  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Closure: </b> This has what I would call a HFN ending...kind of <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[they hadn't even shared "ILYs" yet <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> There are a lot of unanswered questions but there is another book, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20272153.Cold_Blooded_Beautiful__Beautiful___2_" title="Cold-Blooded Beautiful (Beautiful, #2) by Christine Zolendz" rel="nofollow noopener">Cold-Blooded Beautiful</a> that is already released and could address them. <br /><br /><b>Safety:</b> This one is probably <u>Not Safe</u> for most safety gang readers<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have technical cheating (see above)<br />- <b>Does </b> have a descriptive sex scene with the H and OW<br />- <b> Does</b> have both the h and H pushing away<br />- <b> Does</b> have a physical separation between the h and H<br />- <b> Does </b> have abuse<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have a HEA ending <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17086293019167248282">4.5 dark, twisted, and emotional stars. I loved this read! i love smart characters, and i love an author that can write an clever, mind bending tale to compliment them.<br/><br/>Two characters, both internally damaged, see right into the heart and mind of one another.         <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer812637325" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8559444644910865658">When characters claimed that they had a “dark” past, I needed to be convinced that what they went through was indeed “dark”. I’m not mocking them for I know that their experiences could/did happen in real life, but the way it was written came off unconvincingly. At first, the hero, Kade, was dangerous, creepy, twisted. I did enjoy how his mind worked. But then, he just became too brooding and boring. It was also obvious that his pov was written by a woman (big turn off!). His transition to being</span>
  <span id="freeText8559444644910865658" style="display:none">When characters claimed that they had a “dark” past, I needed to be convinced that what they went through was indeed “dark”. I’m not mocking them for I know that their experiences could/did happen in real life, but the way it was written came off unconvincingly. At first, the hero, Kade, was dangerous, creepy, twisted. I did enjoy how his mind worked. But then, he just became too brooding and boring. It was also obvious that his pov was written by a woman (big turn off!). His transition to being nice was unnatural and all too sudden as well or it felt like he became a totally different person. There was some spark of chemistry between him and Lainey/Sam, but it didn’t combust to a full blown fire. Just like a spark, it vanished too fast. <br /><br />There were also parts that were cheesy and ridiculous or if not, the timing was off. The heroine was sometimes annoying and rude. Seriously, I could go on and on... But why suffer through the torture of relieving what I had read when I could be moving on to a much worthier book? Indeed it had some moments, but the bottom line was it just fell flat for me…<br /></span>

<div id="review_814144990" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/814144990" />
    <a title="Karen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6972914-karen"><img alt="Karen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1529600203p2/6972914.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/814144990?book_show_action=true">Jan 06, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Karen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Karen" href="/user/show/6972914-karen">Karen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer814144990" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12540162943518507447"><b>3.5 STARS</b><br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390759870i/8274689._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>Life is tough; you have to endure the bad with the good, because the alternative is so... final. I will endure this...</i>
</b><br/><br/>This is a heartbreaking love story of two people who were both living through the aftermath of separate but both horrifically violent pasts. Each one having their soul charred beyond recognition, and trying to find a way to keep on living with what was left. Two hearts beating separately, yet drawn together by a darkness so intense that only by connecting the two co</span>
  <span id="freeText12540162943518507447" style="display:none"><b>3.5 STARS</b><br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390759870i/8274689._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>Life is tough; you have to endure the bad with the good, because the alternative is so... final. I will endure this...</i>
</b><br><br>This is a heartbreaking love story of two people who were both living through the aftermath of separate but both horrifically violent pasts. Each one having their soul charred beyond recognition, and trying to find a way to keep on living with what was left. Two hearts beating separately, yet drawn together by a darkness so intense that only by connecting the two could they find their way back into the light. <br><br><b>Samantha Matthews</b> was on the run… with her best friend. Trying to escape a past she had no choice but to leave behind. It was a matter of survival… so she had to be careful. In her mad dash to flee, she had to steer clear of police and even the medical treatment she so badly needed. So it was even more of a surprise, when her brief stop to use the restroom at a strip-club bar in the middle of bum-fuck nowhere turns into a crossroads in her life that could change everything.<br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Women/Jennifer-Connelly-jennifer-connelly-205613_1024_768.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390759870i/8274688._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo Jennifer-Connelly-jennifer-connelly-205613_1024_768.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>For it is here, that she will meet <b>
  <i>him</i>
</b>. This enigma of dark secrets that jump starts her heart back to life. But it can’t be… that part of her has been dead for a long time… and what is dead cannot be brought back. <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390759870i/8274692._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Kade Grayson</b> lost his life when he was sixteen. It was horrific. It was tragic. And he relives it every minute of every day. Never to forget. Never to recover. Everyone else has moved on from it, but he cannot. So he exploits it. He revels in it. He shares it with the world and feeds their morbid hunger for it. But still, it does not heal him. He is broken.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390759870i/8274690._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Until he see them… those green eyes… the doors to his long lost soul. But he soon finds that behind those doors live monsters, different but not less horrible than his own. He should steer clear, no… he should RUN the other way. Yet he’s drawn to them, helpless to resist, even if they end up destroying what’s left of him.<br> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390759870i/8274691._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"I'm falling in love with you Sam, and I'm going to let you destroy me."</i>
</b><br><br><br>This book was an incredibly creative love story of two people who were both damaged by the violence of their pasts. I found the author did an amazing job creating intrigue and mystery around the lives of the characters. And the stories that created their pasts were shocking and horrific, yet told in an incredibly emotional and heart wrenching way. I could easily empathize with each if them, and eagerly hoped they would be able to heal each other, and find love together. <br><br><b>
  <i>"His smile...his smile almost killed me. Arrow right to the heart, with a stampede of fluttering butterflies exploding from it."</i>
</b><br><br>I feel torn in my rating of the book. There were parts where I couldn’t fathom giving it anything less than 5 stars, but then I would find myself distracted by overused descriptive terms… I think I mentioned a few in my updates.<br><br><br><b>
  <i>RAW... PRIMAL... VISCERAL... <br><br>DANGEROUS... SAVAGE... FEROCIOUS...</i>
</b> <br><br>OK, I got it.<br> <br>I also felt that the flow of the story was often interrupted. I almost felt like the author took a break… then picked up with something different when returning to the writing. Like the events following what had been previously happening did not fit the situation. At all. This happened several times, and the event that usually fell into place awkwardly would usually be a particularly graphic sex scene. <br><br>Now, the chemistry between these two characters was definitely intense and the sexual experiences they shared appropriately expressed this intensity. I think I just found a few of their encounters to be ill-timed in the story. <br><br>And lastly, I was a bit surprised that a character like Sam, aka Lainey, would be so instantly attracted to another mysterious man with an intensely DARK personality. I mean this woman was very intelligent. It shocks me that she would tangle with another dangerous “bad” boy, when she was still currently running from one. <br><br><b>
  <i>"BAD written all the fuck over it. This...is just a morbid filled ice cream cone dipped in psycho flavored sprinkles."</i>
</b><br><br>But all in all, I still found myself quite drawn into the story and hoping these two could find some peace for themselves. And I’m happy to hear there will be more to come in another book.<br><br>I am a big fan of Christine Zolendz, I think she is an extremely talented and creative writer. And I am anxious to hear more from these characters!!! <br><br><b>3.5 STARS!!!</b><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="12540162943518507447" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_814142967" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/814142967" />
    <a title="AJ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3143126-aj"><img alt="AJ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406382884p2/3143126.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/814142967?book_show_action=true">Jan 06, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AJ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AJ" href="/user/show/3143126-aj">AJ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=duet">duet</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=drama">drama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=dark-n-gritty">dark-n-gritty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer814142967" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6485766542617328593"><b>
  <i>“I’m falling in love with you … and I’m going to let you destroy me.”</i>
</b><br/><br/>Christine Zolendz cements her spot on my list of ‘must read’ authors with this one! I am a MASSIVE fan of Christine’s <i>Mad World</i> series, but she seems to have taken this one to another level, giving us a disturbingly dark and sexy story which is both mature and intelligent, and blended fantastically with sarcastic humour, drama, suspense and a deeply intense romance. Very different from a lot of other romance books out there</span>
  <span id="freeText6485766542617328593" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>“I’m falling in love with you … and I’m going to let you destroy me.”</i>
</b><br /><br />Christine Zolendz cements her spot on my list of ‘must read’ authors with this one! I am a MASSIVE fan of Christine’s <i>Mad World</i> series, but she seems to have taken this one to another level, giving us a disturbingly dark and sexy story which is both mature and intelligent, and blended fantastically with sarcastic humour, drama, suspense and a deeply intense romance. Very different from a lot of other romance books out there, I was hooked from the very first page. <br /><br />Lainey is hiding dark and violent secrets. She is on the run from her old life, and she and her best friend have set themselves up in a small mountain town where they have set about creating new lives for themselves. I love Lainey! She is feisty, with a brilliantly sarcastic sense of humour, and although she has clearly been through hell, she isn’t prepared to put up with any crap from anybody, and I loved her sass.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“If I’m not good enough because I’m a waitress, don't settle for me, don't sink down to my level. You don't deserve anything I have to offer. Let that shit hurt for a hot minute, simmer in it then leave me the fuck alone.”</i>
</blockquote><br />Kade is “<i>rage personified</i>”, a snarky and antisocial recluse, he writes horror novels – his way of dwelling in his anger and “<i>living in a world of lies</i>”, creating fictitious characters he can control only to destroy them. He is described as “<i>savage</i>” and “<i>scary</i>”, and simply put, he is an asshole, and he absolutely owns it. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“Will you call me? Maybe we could go out some time,” she smiled, walking to my front door. <br />“Love, I don’t even remember your name, and I don’t plan on asking you for it again.” <br />“You’re an asshole, you know that?” <br />“Yes, and you’re the whore who let me stick my dick in you and spank your ass,” I said, closing the door on her surprised expression. I would say I cared, but I hated lying. </i>
</blockquote><br />Yeah, I totally fell for him! Of course he’s gorgeous, but he has a brutally violent and tragic past, and is wrestling with hideous demons. His past is hinted at, but when it is completely uncovered, my heart broke for him, and I could absolutely understand how it made him into the man that he is. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>Once you felt violence, most people couldn’t cope with it, they couldn’t even push the words through their lips. It instantly freezes the images in your mind, and those images are indestructible. Then there are people like me, who have been touched by violence so deeply that they completely lose their soul to it.</i>
</blockquote><br />From the moment that Lainey and Kade meet there is insta-lust, epic banter, and a whole heap of eye fuckery going on. I love that the story is told in dual POV, because there are so many conflicting emotions between these two! Clearly there is chemistry, but they have a genuine animosity towards each other as well, and I loved being able to see behind their actions to what was really going on between them.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“I needed to see her again. I needed her to hate me and to stay far away from me, because I wanted to consume her completely.”</i>
  <br />
  <br />
  <i> “I think I finally found someone whose demons would play nice with my own.” </i>
</blockquote><br />Kade and Lainey are deeply tormented souls, and their stories shocked and horrified me. They are sensationally fleshed-out characters, and the different ways that they live with what they’ve been through, and how it has shaped them, is beautifully depicted, and creates some fantastic fireworks in their developing relationship, bringing a level of complexity to it that makes it all so much more intense. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i> “I didn’t care who or what Lainey was, I just wanted her completely. Never in my sick life did I ever give a bit of hope about finding a person who was compatible, who could find comfort in someone as fucking twisted as me.”</i>
  <br />
  <br />
  <i>“No matter how badly it was going to hurt, I didn't want to be anywhere but with Lainey. Let her crush me. Let her destroy me. There wasn't much good left of me, but I wanted her to take every last bit.”</i>
</blockquote><br />The build-up is brimming with sexual tension, and the emotion between them is powerful, and I felt it all along with them. And it all culminates in hotness and romance that left my heart pounding. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> “Everything that happened…to me…is stained here,” I whispered, touching my hand to my heart. “It will forever be in my heart, but what I want … is to move it over a little so I can fit you in there too.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />But how will their all-consuming passion for each other compete with their devastating secrets, and the fact that their horrific pasts are still very much a part of their present? <br /><br />Beautifully written, the story is well paced, full of emotion, and had me madly flipping pages. I love that I was surprised by aspects of the story, and thought that the whole thing played out really cleverly. The ending felt a little bit over dramatic at times, and while the book does not have a cliffhanger, the story is definitely not over. I was actually surprised that the book finished where it did, but I loved the epilogue, and thought that it was a really unique idea – it ties in really nicely with the story, providing a bit more depth to an ending that seemed a little bit abrupt. Of course at the time I was reading it, I didn’t realise that there was going to be a sequel, so I’m now looking forward to learning even more about these complex, damaged characters, as well as seeing where the story goes from here. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“This…this is just a morbid filled ice cream cone dipped in psycho flavored sprinkles.”</i>
</blockquote><br />4.5 stars. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6485766542617328593" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText16032242483450975057" style="display:none"><b>5 Brutally Beautiful Stars</b><br><br><b>A dark twisted read, beautifully written and somewhat poetic</b><br><br>I read Brutally Beautiful a few weeks ago and I wished I wrote my review right when I finished, so this won’t be your typical review, which kills me because I loved it so much.<br><br><b>Short version of the summary</b><br><br>Sam and her best friend are on the run, you don’t know why, but they are beaten up, bruised and battered. We just know they left a terrible situation and both are ready to move forward with their lives. They arrive at a strip joint in the middle of nowhere and both girls get jobs waitressing. Kade, the owner of the strip club is very attracted to Sam, but both Sam and Kade have dark pasts which constantly haunt them. <br><br><b>My Overall Opinion</b><br><br>The beginning starts out with a <b>BAM!</b> both girls are in their car and they are just driving. Both are bloody, hurt and just looking for the next destination. My imitated response was, wow, this is going to be a good book and what happened to these girls, who caused them to run like that?!<br><br>Then they reach a STRIP CLUB! Oh god, it couldn’t have gotten better than that.<br><br>BUT IT DID … BECAUSE OF ….<br><br><b>KADE</b>…. Soown….<br><br>I love me a dark mysterious man. I love me a dark mysterious man who is really really really really mysterious. Kade is kind of just a big question mark and you wanted to unravel his layers and figure out his past.<br><br>ALSO, you know I love me a damsel in distress storyline. This is my second book by Christine Zolendz and she did not disappoint. NOT ONE BIT!<br><br>Sorry I couldn’t give you any more details. Just know it was a fun twisted read. <br><br>As for the ending, there’s a closed cliffy.<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20271650.Brutally_Beautiful__Beautiful___1_" title="Brutally Beautiful (Beautiful, #1) by Christine Zolendz" rel="nofollow noopener">

I also loved the interactions between her and Kade. The dark, deep emotions that he felt for Lainey were so intense. <br /><br /><b>

</b><br /><br /><b>

</b><br /><br /><b>

Christine Zolendz is one of my most favorite authors; she is an amazing story-teller. I will read anything she writes without question!<br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_1527397602" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1527397602" />
    <a title="Ashleyjo" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/33970054-ashleyjo"><img alt="Ashleyjo" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1466919724p2/33970054.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1527397602?book_show_action=true">Jan 27, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ashleyjo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ashleyjo" href="/user/show/33970054-ashleyjo">Ashleyjo</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1527397602" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17544853681671610688"><br/>Thank you to the lovely friend that loaned me these books:) xoxo! <br/><br/>Ehh, this is a difficult book for me tag with a rating because it's both great and meh. 4 stars for first half ....2 stars for second half.... 0 stars for the end = 2 stars overall. <br/><br/><b> Basic Plot </b> <br/><br/>Two women hit the road beaten and bloodied. Hours later, they stop at a small town and end up deciding it's as good as any place to hide from <i>whatever </i> hell they're running from. <br/><br/>The friend and bar owner fall into a relationship, further t</span>
  <span id="freeText17544853681671610688" style="display:none"><br>Thank you to the lovely friend that loaned me these books:) xoxo! <br><br>Ehh, this is a difficult book for me tag with a rating because it's both great and meh. 4 stars for first half ....2 stars for second half.... 0 stars for the end = 2 stars overall. <br><br><b> Basic Plot </b> <br><br>Two women hit the road beaten and bloodied. Hours later, they stop at a small town and end up deciding it's as good as any place to hide from <i>whatever </i> hell they're running from. <br><br>The friend and bar owner fall into a relationship, further tethering them to the town. <br><br>A complicated, explosive relationship develops between the FMC &amp; her new employer's brother. Both are angry, love to throw verbal knives at each other, are hiding from the world, and are very damaged by the past. <br><br>Him... <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453910623i/17890060.jpg" width="250" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Her... <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453910623i/17890061.jpg" width="250" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Can these damaged souls find comfort and peace together because they each understand the other's demons? Will they kill each other first? Or, will the very demons they sense within each other as a place of understanding and acceptance be what actually reignites the other's past fears? <br><br><b>Initial Thoughts </b> <br><br>This is the kind of story and characters that jump off the pages into your brain; swims around to find that alpha neuron; and then attaches the scene, the characters, &amp; the sentiment there so the rest of your brain knows your ass has just been <i> owned</i> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453910623i/17890062.jpg" width="250" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>The character &amp; plot development is spectacular for the first half of the book. I'm entranced by the characters personalities and pasts. <br><br>Him... <br><br><blockquote>
<br><br>"I live in a world of lies, fictitious characters I dream up and breathe life into, just to break, for the enjoyment of horror readers throughout the world." <br><br>"Words had always come easily to me. Violence and hate were in my veins. I was rage personified, and horror and malice were my only friends. We had lived together peacefully since I came to terms with being me." <br><br>
</blockquote> <br><br>Her... <br><br><blockquote>"To hell with him, my skin was way too tough for some pathetic gorilla in a Gucci suit to break through." <br><br>"I was too old to play games. I was too messed up with my own issues to care about his, and I didn't do drama, not even in TV."<br><br>
</blockquote> <br><br>This book begins with multi-faceted characters who are as witty and leveled as they are completely f'd up and kookoo. <br><br>Sadly.... <br><br><b>The Car Stalls </b> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453910623i/17890063._SX540_.jpg" width="250" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br> <br>This story stalls for me and the characters fall into this angsty push and pull slump of recycle, rinse, and repeat that doesn't even ring true to their type A personalities. <br><br>He is obsessed with her and it pisses him off. So he verbally assaults her, drinks, stalks, verbally assaults, drinks, stalks - wash and repeat. <br><br>She has her own demons chasing her &amp; doesn't have time to try and fix anyone else's... Or does she... Or doesn't she.. Or does she... Or doesn't she.. &gt;&gt; you get the point. <br><br>^ This just goes on too long before suddenly transitioning to <i>love</i> WITH no substance other than <i> my damage matches your damage. </i> IF I have to listen to this type of inner dialogue and witness this type of angst, there better be a damn good substantive climax and resolve. <br><br><b>Where Was The Climax? </b> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382369535ra/5851484.gif" width="250" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>There's a tense moment when the MCs past seems to have possibly caught up with her, but this just isn't the peak or climax to the storyline that I'm expecting. Some of her cards are laid out on the table, but nothing the reader hasn't already guessed by this point. So, this just isn't <i> that big moment. </i> <br><br>There's a very long and detailed scene where he describes his trauma and inner thoughts to the FMC. It's excellently written to make you feel the MMC's pain and anger, but, again, it's just not that climatic moment that pushes the story forward that I was expecting. She shares nothing. She concedes nothing. So, still not <i> that big moment. </i> <br><br>That's not to say there aren't quite a few profound statements, like her "redefine normal" line and a girl power bathroom scene. There are plenty of fist bump lines. <br><br>There are some laugh and snort out loud lines, too. <br><br>But...<br><br><b> By The End </b> <br><br>I feel like the guts of the story became too diluted &amp; sparsely spread by the rinse and repeat and absence of that climax to push it forward. <br><br><b> Don't <u>Blackmail </u> Me Into Reading Book 2... Make Me <u>Want </u> To Read It! <br></b> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1453910623ra/17890064.gif" width="250" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>The sudden transition from run absentmindedly to run with a plan was odd and felt like author' blackmail. <br><br>The answer to her problem was convoluted and plucked from the clear blue sky.<br><br>There's no discussion till the plot line just abruptly changes and the reader is in the throes of something where the how, why, when, where, who was NEVER even mentioned. She wasnt going to share her past and was going to run, and then BAM something different and complicated with no discussion. <br><br>^^ Odd. Unbelievable. Cloak and dagger to blackmail you into reading book two. Leaving out shit between scene jumps for no reason other than to keep you in the dark and tell you later. Uhm, no! That '-aha, guess what we did between chapter x &amp; y and didn't tell you about' ... 'Guess you'll have to read book two to possibly find out' kinda shit DOES NOT work for me! <br><br>There's still a lot of mystery surrounding the FMC's past to help readers want to read book two. We've barely scratched her surface, and that's really the only thing that makes me want to read on. My patience is very, very thin at this point, and if the cloak and dagger routine from book one isn't immediately cleared up, then I will shut that mfer and be DONE! <br><br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="17544853681671610688" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('d1tVVzs02A8Lbue2o/YLafuKMUwow1gLSVxHjuBTOSBQndkvGI1WMSjdJjZ8RPDQzROJv8E/IzMuEBnLaLjC1g==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Uuf9rhbqBzmIJcC9ZIAe8e+cjw/kFUIu5bMbrCGAtGF1IXHWNVOJB6uWAT27MuVI2QU3/A3pORaC/0XpqWtPlw==')})
  }
